# Plot Events

# Blackmail									7250-7270
# Drunken Plot Member						7040-7045

# Ultimatum event series					8000-8040
# Plot to kill character 					8220-8227

# Assassination notification events			8250-8299
#											7700-7999


###########################################
# Blackmail
###########################################
# 7250-7270

##########################################
#Buy loyalty plot (by knuckey)
namespace = plot_event

# The plot has been leaked
character_event = {
	id = 7250
	desc = "EVTDESC7250"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
			has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
			has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
			has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
			has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
			has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
			has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
			has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
		}
		is_plot_active = no
		num_of_plot_backers = 1
		job_spymaster = {
			NOT = { is_plot_target_of = PREV }
		}
		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				OR = { higher_tier_than = baron is_patrician = yes }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { any_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_blackmailed } }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { #CK2+
		months = 120

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_imbecile_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_dumb_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7250"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			top_liege = {
				random_realm_lord = {
					limit = {
						OR = { higher_tier_than = baron is_patrician = yes }

						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = ROOT } }
						NOT = { any_liege = { character = ROOT } }
						employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_blackmailed } }
					}
					letter_event = { id = 7255 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail or not
letter_event = {
	id = 7255
	desc = "EVTDESC7255"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7260 days = 1 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7260" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail attempt
letter_event = {
	id = 7260
	desc = "EVTDESC7260"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7260"
		wealth = -100
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7265 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7260"
		set_character_flag = abort_plot
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = { #CK2+
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = scheming_bastard
						months = 120
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7270 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail succeded
letter_event = {
	id = 7265
	desc = "EVTDESC7265"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		treasury = 100
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_blackmailed
			who = FROM
			months = 120
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail failed
letter_event = {
	id = 7270
	desc = "EVTDESC7270"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7270"
	}
}


###########################################
# Drunken Plot Member
###########################################
# 7040-7045

# Drunk plot member spills the beans
character_event = {
	id = 7040
	desc = "EVTDESC7040"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
				has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
				has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
				has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
				has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
				has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
				has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
				has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
				has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
			NOT = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { #CK2+
		months = 1000

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_imbecile_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_dumb_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7040"
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
					has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
					has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
					has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
					has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
					has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
					has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
					has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
					has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
				NOT = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7040
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7045 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7045
	desc = "EVTDESC7045"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7045"
		set_character_flag = abort_plot
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = { NOT = { character = PREV } }
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = devious_plotter
						months = 120
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - seniority
letter_event = {
	id = 8005
	desc = "EVTDESC8005"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_seniority }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_seniority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { culture = summer_islander }
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_seniority = { # The target (title) of the faction
				succession = seniority
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								agnatic_culture_trigger = yes
								true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes
								enatic_culture_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
					gender_succ = cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { agnatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = agnatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = true_cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { enatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
				}
			}
		}
		recalc_succession = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
						AND = {
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8076 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8055 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
					letter_event = { id = 8075 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8005"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				culture = summer_islander
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {
						same_liege = ROOT
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8105 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - primogeniture
letter_event = {
	id = 8010
	desc = "EVTDESC8010"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_primogeniture }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = andal
						culture_group = first_men
						culture_group = dornish
					}
				}
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_primogeniture = { # The target (title) of the faction
				succession = primogeniture
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								agnatic_culture_trigger = yes
								true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes
								enatic_culture_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
					gender_succ = cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { agnatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = agnatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = true_cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { enatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
				}
			}
		}
		recalc_succession = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
						AND = {
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8081 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8060 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
					letter_event = { id = 8080 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					culture_group = andal
					culture_group = first_men
					culture_group = dornish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {
						same_liege = ROOT
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8110 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - feudal elective
letter_event = {
	id = 8015
	desc = "EVTDESC8015"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_elective_culture_religion_trigger = no
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_feudal_elective = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_law_potential = succ_kingsmoot_elective
					}
					add_law_w_cooldown = succ_kingsmoot_elective
				}
				else = {
					add_law_w_cooldown = succ_feudal_elective
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								agnatic_culture_trigger = yes
								true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes
								enatic_culture_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
					gender_succ = cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { agnatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = agnatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = true_cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { enatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
					gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
				}
			}
		}
		recalc_succession = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
						AND = {
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8086 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8065 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective
					letter_event = { id = 8085 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_elective_culture_religion_trigger = no
				#kingdom must be primary, or have many ironborn high lords
				FROM = {
					faction_succ_feudal_elective = {
						OR = {
							is_primary_holder_title = yes
							any_de_jure_vassal_title = {
								count = 5
								higher_tier_than = COUNT
								holder_scope = {
									has_elective_culture_religion_trigger = yes
									NOT = { character = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {
						same_liege = ROOT
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8115 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective
				tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {

						}

							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}

		}

# Ultimatum - crown authority
letter_event = {
	id = 8025
	desc = "EVTDESC8025"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_lower_crown_authority }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			faction_lower_crown_authority = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_1 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_0
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_2 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_3 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_2
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_4 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_3
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
						AND = {
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8094 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8067 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
					letter_event = { id = 8095 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_lowered_crown_authority
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {
						same_liege = ROOT
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8117 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - gain a vassal title
letter_event = {
	id = 8030
	desc = "EVTDESC8030"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 0.66 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
							liege = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { character = PREV }
								OR = {
									opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_married = ROOT
									primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
									trait = just
									FROM = { #aggressive expansion
										relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
										any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

				}

		}

			}

						trait = dragon_rider
						any_friend = {
							trait = dragon
							martial = 10
							NOT = { trait = maimed_dragon }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege

					NOT = { character = ROOT }

						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT

						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {

						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative power

				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 3 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8

# Regent responds to crown authority ultimatum
letter_event = {
	id = 8026
	desc = "EVTDESC8026"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_lower_crown_authority }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 33 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 66 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 99 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							#strong loyalists
							AND = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
								any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
							}
						}
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							liege = {
								NOT = { character = PREV }
								OR = {
									opinion = { who = PREV value = 20 }
									dynasty = PREV
									is_married = PREV
									primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
									trait = just
									FROM = { #aggressive expansion
										relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
										any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				faction_lower_crown_authority = { # The target (title) of the faction
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = centralization_1 }
						add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_0
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = centralization_2 }
						add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_1
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = centralization_3 }
						add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_2
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = centralization_4 }
						add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			liege = {
				change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
				hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
				any_player = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_liege_or_above = PREV
							is_liege_of = PREV
							dynasty = PREV
							is_close_relative = PREV
							is_married = PREV
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = PREV
							is_allied_with = PREV
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
							AND = {
								is_within_diplo_range = PREV
								PREV = { tier = EMPEROR }
							}
							character = PREV
						}
						NOR = {
							character = FROM
							FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = 8094 }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8067 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
					letter_event = { id = 8095 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
			liege = { character_event = { id = plot_event.502 } }
		}
		FROM = {

			}

# Ultimatum - Independence
letter_event = {
	id = 8035
	desc = "EVTDESC8035"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_independence }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_independence
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000" # Fold to demand
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
						AND = {
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8093 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8069 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_independence
					letter_event = { id = 8097 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_independence
				set_defacto_liege = THIS
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}

		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_granted_independence
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }

					trait = brave

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8119 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_independence
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 0.33 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						15 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						35 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - Install Pretender
letter_event = {
	id = 8036
	desc = "EVTDESC8036"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_claimant }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_claimant
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					supported_claimant = {
						NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					supported_claimant = {
						NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				supported_claimant = {
					ROOT_FROM = {
						supported_claimant_title = {
							usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals = { target = PREVPREV type = claim }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8099 }
			}
			FROM = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_claimant
					letter_event = { id = 8098 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				letter_event = { id = 8061 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Has powerful ally
				any_allied_character = {
					is_ruler = yes
					relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
					OR = {
						same_liege = ROOT
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8111 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner

# Demand accepted - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8061
	desc = "EVTDESC8061"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		supported_claimant = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		supported_claimant = {
			hidden_tooltip = { #This stops wars to depose liege
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = installed_pretender
					duration = 10
					hidden = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = supported_claimant
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = yes
					host = { character = FROM  }
				}
				prisoner = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #If patrician enforcing claim on republic hold election in their favour
					is_patrician = yes
					FROM = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
					liege = { character = FROM }
					ROOT = { supported_claimant_title = { is_primary_holder_title = yes } }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					prestige = 75000
					FROM = { character_event = { id = REP.903 tooltip = TOOLTIPREP.903 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				ROOT = {
					supported_claimant_title = {
						# If the claimant has the wrong government type, take care of that first.
						if = {
							limit = {
								higher_tier_than = event_target:supported_claimant
								holder_scope = {
									OR = {
										is_tribal = yes
										is_feudal = yes
										is_nomadic = yes
									}
								}
								event_target:supported_claimant = {
									is_ruler = yes
									OR = {
										is_theocracy = yes
										is_republic = yes
									}
								}
							}
							event_target:supported_claimant = {
								hidden_tooltip = { #Universal on death/abdication event
									if = {
										limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
										set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
									}
									set_character_flag = abdication
									character_event = { id = 45341 }
									clr_character_flag = abdication
									clr_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
								}
								abdicate = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								holder_scope = { has_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars }
								#tier = KING
							}
							event_target:supported_claimant = { set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								holder_scope = {
									OR = {
										has_character_flag = supporting_king
										has_character_flag = neutral
										has_character_flag = against_king
										has_character_flag = rebel_leader
									}
								}
								#tier = KING
							}
							event_target:supported_claimant = { set_character_flag = neutral }
						}
						tooltip = { usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals = { target = event_target:supported_claimant type = claim } }
						if = { #Don't want ousted person to steal a vassal's title
							limit = {
								holder_scope = {
									tier = PREV #Only if primary tier title
									OR = {
										NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
										NOT = { #also do this if only military commands left
											any_demesne_title = {
												tier = COUNT
												location = { is_capital = no }
												NOT = { has_title_flag = military_command }
											}
										}
									}
									OR = {	#pretender is...
										event_target:supported_claimant = { NOT = { demesne_size = 1 } } #unlanded
										AND =  { #small baron
											event_target:supported_claimant = { tier = BARON }
											PREV = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
										}
										capital_scope = { county = { event_target:supported_claimant = { has_claim = PREV } } } #has claim on capital
									}
									OR = { #Must be related in some way
										dynasty = event_target:supported_claimant
										is_close_relative = event_target:supported_claimant
										capital_scope = { county = { event_target:supported_claimant = { has_claim = PREV } } }
									}
								}
							}
							holder_scope = {
								transfer_scaled_wealth = { to = event_target:supported_claimant value = all }
								abdicate_to = event_target:supported_claimant
							}
							add_pressed_claim = ROOT_FROM
							ROOT_FROM = {
								opinion = { who = event_target:supported_claimant	 modifier = opinion_usurped_title }
							}
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { event_target:supported_claimant = { is_ruler = yes } }
								holder_scope = { opinion = { who = event_target:supported_claimant	 modifier = opinion_usurped_title } }
								gain_title = { target = event_target:supported_claimant type = claim } #usurp_title sometimes takes all titles for some reason
								add_pressed_claim = ROOT_FROM
							}
							if = {
								limit = { event_target:supported_claimant = { is_ruler = no } }
								usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = event_target:supported_claimant type = claim }
							}
						}

						hidden_tooltip = {
							if = {
								limit = { holder_scope = { has_character_flag = neutral } }
								holder_scope = { any_vassal = { set_character_flag = neutral } }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { title = e_iron_throne } #Lose crownlands
								holder_scope = { character_event = { id = maintenance.37 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = maintenance.26 } #Vanilla bug resets laws, so fix empire tracker law and primogeniture
			character_event = { id = maintenance.21 } #Take dejure vassals if King title usurped
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_close_relative = PREV
						NOT = { age = 16 }
					}
					move_character = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = rebel_leader
					e_iron_throne = {
						holder_scope = { NOT = { war_with = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				remove_trait = rebel_leader
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = regency.55 days = 2 } } #Become Regent if possible
	}
}

# Demand accepted - Independence
letter_event = {
	id = 8069
	desc = "EVTDESC8069"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				controls_religion = no
				tier = ROOT
				NOT = {
					dejure_liege_title = {
						OR = {
							FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
							dejure_liege_title = {
								OR = {
									FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
									dejure_liege_title = { FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_weak_pressed_claim = FROM
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = mega_wars.50 } #Character wins indep war maintenance
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_independence_ultimatum_taken
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_faction_won"
				duration = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = 8097
	desc = "EVTDESC8097"

	show_from_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = ROOT
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					dejure_liege_title = {
						OR = {
							FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
							dejure_liege_title = {
								OR = {
									FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
									dejure_liege_title = { FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_weak_pressed_claim = FROM
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = mega_wars.50 } #Character wins indep war maintenance
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "GOOD"
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_grateful
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 5
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_granted_independence
			who = FROM
			months = 120
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_faction_won"
				duration = 10
			}
			character_event = { id = mega_wars.54 days = 1 } #AI lesser lords get vassalised
		}
	}
}

# Demand rejected - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8111
	desc = "EVTDESC8100"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { #check for blackfyre support
				limit = {
					faction_claimant = {
						title = e_iron_throne
						holder_scope = { NOT = { dynasty = 57 } }
					}
					supported_claimant = {
						dynasty = 57
						age = 14
						prisoner = no
						OR = {
							has_landed_title = d_golden_company
							d_golden_company = { holder_scope = { opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = 0 } } }
							AND = {
								d_golden_company = { holder_scope = { opinion = { who = PREVPREV value = -25 } } }
								NOT = { #oldest male
									any_dynasty_member = {
										dynasty = 57
										prisoner = no
										can_press_claims_trigger = yes

										is_female = no
										NOT = { trait = bastard }
										OR = {
											AND = {
												sibling = PREV
												is_older_than = PREV
											}
											any_child = { character = PREVPREV }
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				clr_global_flag = blackfyre_invasion
				supported_claimant = { save_event_target_as = blackfyre_supported_claimant }
				d_golden_company = { holder_scope = { character_event = { id = invasions.600 days = 7 } } }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				supported_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_unsafe_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					supported_claimant = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #If external ruler flag as such so top liege can intervene
				limit = {
					supported_claimant = {
						is_ruler = yes
						independent = no
						NOT = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = external_claimant
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				supported_claimant = {
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_supported_claimant
						years = 100
					}
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_unsafe_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = other_claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
		}
	}
}

# POISONED WINE - ADULTS ONLY

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8150
	desc = "EVTDESC8150"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				has_opinion_modifier = { #Attending plotter's wedding
					modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
					who = ROOT
				}
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { #Hosting wedding
					modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
					who = ROOT
				}
				AND = { #Attending plotter's feast
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					ROOT = { has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast is_liege_of = ROOT }
				}
				AND = { #Hosting feast
					has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = guest_feast_started liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
				AND = { #Attending the same wedding
					ROOT = {
						any_liege = {
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
								modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
								who = ROOT
							}
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
								modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
								who = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { #Attending the same feast
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					liege = {
						has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
						any_vassal = { character = ROOT }
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					}
				}
			}
			is_incapable = no
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {

			plot_power = 0.5
		}

			plot_power = 1.0
		}

			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}

			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {

# A plot backer sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8151
	desc = "EVTDESC8151"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				is_incapable = no
				OR = {
					at_location = ROOT # The Plotter needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
					has_opinion_modifier = { #Attending plotter's wedding
						modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
						who = ROOT
					}
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { #Hosting wedding
						modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
						who = ROOT
					}
					AND = { #Attending plotter's feast
						has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
						ROOT = { has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast is_liege_of = ROOT }
					}
					AND = { #Hosting feast
						has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
						ROOT = { has_character_flag = guest_feast_started liege = { character = ROOT } }
					}
					AND = { #Attending the same wedding
						ROOT = {
							any_liege = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
									modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
									who = ROOT
								}
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
									modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
									who = PREVPREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = { #Attending the same feast
						has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
						liege = {
							has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
							any_vassal = { character = ROOT }
						}
						ROOT = {
							has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character

				ROOT = {

# Poisoned Wine - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8155
	desc = "EVTDESC8155"
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		prisoner = no

		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = food_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = food_murder
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8155" # Drinks the wine
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8156 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8157 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8155" # Discovers the poison
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {

					}
					modifier = {

# Poisoned Wine - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8156
	desc = "EVTDESC8156"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8156
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_poison
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_poison
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8158
	desc = "EVTDESC8158"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
				reveal_plot = yes
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
				reveal_plot = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8158"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}
