# Poisoned Wine - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8163
	desc = "EVTDESC8163"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# FALLING ACCIDENT - CHILDREN ONLY

# Falling accident - The plotter sees an opportunity
character_event = {
	id = 8170
	desc = "EVTDESC8170"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			NOT = { age = 16 }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			is_incapable = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3600

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8170" # The conspirators provide the poison
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8182 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8175 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8175" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8170" # Bribe a Guard
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8182 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8175 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8175" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8170" # Bribe a Guard
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8182 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8175 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8175" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC8170" # I know just the person for the job...
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8182 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8175 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8175" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Falling Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8175
	desc = "EVTDESC8175"
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		prisoner = no

		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8175" # Falls
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8176 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8177 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8175" # Dodges
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8178 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8179 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = "EVTOPTA8176"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falling Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8178
	desc = "EVTDESC8178"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8178"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {

			plot_target_title = { save_event_target_as = weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
		}
	}

	option = { #Yes
		name = "EVTOPTA7500"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3

				factor = 0

						trait = envious

					NOT = { trait = just }

					trait = just

				}
				NAND = { #I'm zealous and target is heathen
					trait = zealous
					event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_target = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } }
				}

					}

			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_agreed_to_split_title months = 60 }
		}
		if = { #PLayer has 30 days to give title
			limit = { ai = no }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIP7504A
				hidden_tooltip = {
					FROM = { plot_target_title = { save_event_target_as = weaken_fellow_vassal_title } }
					capital_scope = {
						province_event = { id = 7512 days = 30 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = { #ai give title to random relative/courtier
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_liege_or_above = ROOT
					OR = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					}
					NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_ruler = no
							OR = {
								ROOT = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										tier = COUNT
										location = { is_capital = no }
										de_jure_liege_or_above = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title
									}
								}
								event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title = { #can grant landless kingdom if capital is owned by a republic
									capital_scope = {
										owner = {
											is_republic = yes
											is_liege_or_above = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						capital_scope = {
							OR = {
								duchy = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
								kingdom = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
							}
						}
					}
					is_incapable = no
					prisoner = no
					OR = {
						is_primary_heir = no
						sibling = ROOT
					}
					can_inherit_titles_trigger = yes
					OR = {
						is_female = no
						ROOT = {
							primary_title = {
								OR = {
									has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
									has_law = enatic_succession
									has_law = true_cognatic_succession
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_female = yes
						ROOT = {
							primary_title = {
								OR = {
									has_law = cognatic_succession
									has_law = agnatic_succession
									has_law = true_cognatic_succession
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
			}
			clear_event_target = chosen_holder
			random_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
					is_friend = ROOT
				}
				save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						ROOT = { trait = familyperson }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = { #If no dynast found, find a friend
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_friend = {
					limit = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
						OR = {
							AND = {
								is_ruler = no
								OR = {
									ROOT = {
										any_demesne_title = {
											tier = COUNT
											location = { is_capital = no }
											de_jure_liege_or_above = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title
										}
									}
									event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title = { #can grant landless kingdom if capital is owned by a republic
										capital_scope = {
											owner = {
												is_republic = yes
												is_liege_or_above = ROOT
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							capital_scope = {
								OR = {
									duchy = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
									kingdom = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
								}
							}
						}
						is_incapable = no
						prisoner = no
						is_primary_heir = no
						can_inherit_titles_trigger = yes
						OR = {
							is_female = no
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									OR = {
										has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
										has_law = enatic_succession
										has_law = true_cognatic_succession
									}
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							is_female = yes
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									OR = {
										has_law = cognatic_succession
										has_law = agnatic_succession
										has_law = true_cognatic_succession
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = { #liked vassal in title
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						is_feudal = yes
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
						capital_scope = {
							OR = {
								duchy = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
								kingdom = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
							}
						}
						is_incapable = no
						prisoner = no
						can_inherit_titles_trigger = yes
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = { #liked courtier
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						is_ruler = no
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
						OR = {
							ROOT = {
								any_demesne_title = {
									tier = COUNT
									location = { is_capital = no }
									de_jure_liege_or_above = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title
								}
							}
							event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title = { #can grant landless kingdom if capital is owned by a republic
								capital_scope = {
									owner = {
										is_republic = yes
										is_liege_or_above = ROOT
									}
								}
							}
						}
						is_incapable = no
						prisoner = no
						can_inherit_titles_trigger = yes
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			if = { #random vassal
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:chosen_holder = { always = yes } } }
				random_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						is_feudal = yes
						capital_scope = {
							OR = {
								duchy = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
								kingdom = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
							}
						}
						can_inherit_titles_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chosen_holder
				}
			}
			event_target:chosen_holder = {
				event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title = {
					capital_scope = {
						if = { #gain capital if holder is a republic
							limit = {
								owner = {
									is_republic = yes
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
									NOT = { character = event_target:chosen_holder }
								}
							}
							owner = { save_event_target_as = republic_leader }
							capital_holding = { save_event_target_as = old_capital_holding }
							random_province_holding = {
								limit = { holding_type = castle }
								gain_title = event_target:chosen_holder
								hidden_tooltip = { province_capital = yes }
							}
							county = { gain_title = event_target:chosen_holder }
							hidden_tooltip = {
								event_target:republic_leader = {
									event_target:old_capital_holding = {
										gain_title = PREV
										event_target:republic_leader = { capital = PREV }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					grant_title = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_kingdom } } }
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_granted_kingdom
					}
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant }
					clr_character_flag = potential_dynast_claimant
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			prestige = -250
		}
		if = {
			limit = { lower_tier_than = KING }
			prestige = -125
		}
	}
	option = { #Never
		name = "EVTOPTB7504"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROMFROM power = 0.1 } }
				NOR = {
					trait = ambitious
					trait = brave
					trait = wroth
					trait = lunatic
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROMFROM power = 0.1 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROMFROM power = 0.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				relative_power = { who = FROMFROM power = 0.4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7509 }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_refused_abdicate_title }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

		}

		}
	}
}

	id = 7506
	desc = "EVTDESC7506"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7506"
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			show_portrait = yes
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				years = 6
			}
			any_plot_backer = { show_portrait = yes }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 10 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = 7507 days = 30 random = 70 } #AI declares war?
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7506"
		trigger = {
			any_backed_character = { character = FROM }
		}
		FROM = {
			plot_target_char = {
				show_portrait = yes
				opinion = {
					modifier = scheming_bastard
					who = ROOT
					years = 6
				}
				tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 10 } }
			}
			any_plot_backer = { show_portrait = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7506"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = FROM
				any_backed_character = { character = FROM }
			}
		}
		show_portrait = FROM
		FROM = {
			plot_target_char = {
				show_portrait = yes
				tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 10 } }
			}
			any_plot_backer = { show_portrait = yes }
		}
	}

	after = {
		tooltip = {
			FROM = { plot_target_char = { change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 10 } } }
		}
	}
}

					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = dragon_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		else = { #find claimants in realm
			any_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_strong_claim = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
						AND = {
							has_weak_claim = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
							event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title = {
								OR = {
									holder_scope = { has_regent = yes }
									OR = {
										AND = {
											OR = {
												has_law = cognatic_succession
												has_law = agnatic_succession
											}
											PREV = { is_female = no }
											holder_scope = { is_female = yes }
										}
										AND = {
											OR = {
												has_law = enatic_succession
												has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
											}
											PREV = { is_female = yes }
											holder_scope = { is_female = no }
										}
									}
									is_contested = yes # Is already being contested in some form of Claim or Succession War
									holder_scope = { trait = bastard }
									holder_scope = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					prisoner = no
				}
				set_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
			}
			random_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
					is_close_relative = ROOT
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = realm_claimant
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							can_use_cb = {
								target = event_target:weaken_vassal_target
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty_title = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title = {
							reverse_war = {
								target = ROOT
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
					dynasty = ROOT
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = realm_claimant
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							can_use_cb = {
								target = event_target:weaken_vassal_target
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty_title = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title = {
							reverse_war = {
								target = ROOT
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = realm_claimant
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							can_use_cb = {
								target = event_target:weaken_vassal_target
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty_title = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title = {
							reverse_war = {
								target = ROOT
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -30 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = realm_claimant
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							can_use_cb = {
								target = event_target:weaken_vassal_target
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty_title = event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						event_target:weaken_vassal_target_title = {
							reverse_war = {
								target = ROOT
								casus_belli = other_claim
								thirdparty = event_target:realm_claimant
							}
						}
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#if no casus belli found, cancel plot
			cancel_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NO
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		cancel_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
	}
	after = {
		any_realm_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
			}
			clr_character_flag = potential_realm_claimant
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7508"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7508"
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7510 }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_made_vassal_split_vassal months = 60 }
			any_plot_backer = {
				letter_event = { id = 7510 }
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_made_vassal_split_vassal months = 60 }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_close_relative = FROM
						dynasty = FROM
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = FROMFROM } }
				}
				character_event = { id = 7510 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = "EVTOPTA7510"
		trigger = {
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			plot_target_char = { character = FROMFROM }
		}
		show_portrait = FROM
		if = { #player has 30 days to give away title
			limit = { FROMFROM = { ai = no } }
			set_character_flag = weakened_fellow_vassal_player_agreed
		}
		else = { set_character_flag = weakened_fellow_vassal }
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = scheming_bastard
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7510"
		trigger = {
			any_backed_character = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
		}
		show_portrait = FROM
		show_portrait = FROMFROMFROM
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = scheming_bastard
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7510"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = FROMFROMFROM } }
			NAND = {
				has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
				plot_target_char = { character = FROMFROM }
			}
		}
		show_portrait = FROM
		show_portrait = FROMFROMFROM
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			any_plot_backer = { show_portrait = yes }
		}
	}
}

# Check player promise
province_event = { #province event , to ensure player gets event on heir if character dies
	id = 7512

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window =  yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title = {
			holder_scope = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							character = ROOT_FROM
							AND = {
								dynasty = ROOT_FROM
								ai = no
							}
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = 7513 }
					break = yes
				}
			}
		}
		#If no broken promise found, plot is successful
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
					plot_target_title = { title = event_target:weaken_fellow_vassal_title }
				}
				set_character_flag = weakened_fellow_vassal
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		FROMFROM = { clr_character_flag = weakened_fellow_vassal_player_agreed }
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = 7513
	desc = "EVTDESC7513"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7513"
		change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROMFROMFROM = { is_alive = yes higher_tier_than = ROOT } }
			FROMFROMFROMFROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_agreed_to_split_title } }
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_agreed_to_split_title }
				}
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } } }
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_agreed_to_split_title } }
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_agreed_to_split_title }
				}
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

	}
}
character_event = {
	id = 7515

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal }
			plot_target_title = {
				holder_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { character = FROM }
							OR = {
								FROM = { is_alive = yes }
								primary_title = { title = PREVPREV }
								NOR = {
									tier = PREV
									num_of_duke_titles = 3
								}
								is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
						ROOT = { set_character_flag = weakened_fellow_vassal }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = checking_for_plot_success
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Archer Ambush
character_event = {
	id = 7700
	desc = "EVTDESC7700"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_ruler = yes
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			is_incapable = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {

				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}

			plot_power = 1.5

			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7700" # The conspirators provide the archers
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}

					character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7700" # Hire archers
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			martial < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {

			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			martial < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7700" # Knows good archers
		tooltip_info = martial
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			martial = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {

			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			martial < 10
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

				plot_power = 1.0
			}

			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8151" # Ask the Plotter for funds

					OR = {

character_event = {
	id = 7705
	desc = "EVTDESC7705"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder

		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}

				25 = {
					modifier = {

			}
		}
	}

				limit = {

						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes

						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }

			}

		hidden_tooltip = {

# Archer Ambush - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7706
	desc = "EVTDESC7706"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7706"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Archer Ambush - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7708
	desc = "EVTDESC7708"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7708"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7713
	desc = "EVTDESC7713"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

### MANURE EXPLOSION
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Manure Explosion
character_event = {
	id = 7720
	desc = "EVTDESC7720"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {

# Manure Explosion - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7725
	desc = "EVTDESC7725"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7725" # Blown up
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}

						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}

						intrigue = 17

					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}

						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }

			}
			if = {

					limit = {

						is_incapable = no

						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }

							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}

# Manure Explosion - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7726
	desc = "EVTDESC7726"
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_house
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7726"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7728
	desc = "EVTDESC7728"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7728"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Backer informs Plotter of plan
character_event = {
	id = 7730
	desc = "EVTDESC7730"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7730"
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7731 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8161" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { character = FROM }
				}
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7733
	desc = "EVTDESC7733"
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_house
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Notification: Failure, and discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7735
	desc = "EVTDESC7735"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7735"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}
	}
}

### INFANTICIDE - INFANTS ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Infanticide
character_event = {
	id = 7740
	desc = "EVTDESC7740"
	picture = GFX_evt_birth
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { age = 5 }
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7740" # The conspirators bribe the maid
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7742 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7745 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7745" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7740" # Bribe maid
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7752 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7745 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7745" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7740" # Bribe maid
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7752 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7745 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7745" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7740" # Knows maid
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7752 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7745 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7745" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# A plot backer sees an opportunity - Infanticide
character_event = {
	id = 7741
	desc = "EVTDESC7741"
	picture = GFX_evt_birth
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				NOT = { age = 5 }
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			}
			OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.10
					}
				}
			}
		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.60
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.70
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV

					}

				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.90
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

	option = {

				plot_power = 1.0

		random_backed_character = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

				plot_power = 1.0
				plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }

		name = "EVTOPTB8151" # Ask the Plotter for funds
		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {

						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0

				}
			}
		}

				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
				plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7742 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8152" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7740" # Bribe maid
		trigger = {
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
					plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
				plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7750 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7740" # Knows maid
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
				plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }
			}
		}

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5

	is_triggered_only = yes

		plot_target_char = { NOT = { age = 5 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7742"
		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
			from = ROOT
			to = FROM
			value = 0.5
			min = 10
			max = 75
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7743 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8153" } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8152"
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7744 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8154" } }

# Infanticide - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7745
	desc = "EVTDESC7745"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
					NOT = { age = 5 }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
						NOT = { age = 5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7745" # Smothered
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7746 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7747 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7745" # Not smothered
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7748 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7749 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}

character_event = {
	id = 7746
	desc = "EVTDESC7746"
	picture = GFX_evt_family
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7746"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7748
	desc = "EVTDESC7748"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7748"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7753
	desc = "EVTDESC7753"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Prison Break
character_event = {
	id = 7760
	desc = "EVTDESC7760"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			prisoner = yes
			OR = { #Can't try this twice
				NOT = { has_character_flag = tried_prison_break }
				had_character_flag = { flag = tried_prison_break days = 1500 }
			}
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}

				power = 0.20
			}
		}

			}

			}
		}
		modifier = {

			}
		}

			plot_power_contribution = {

				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7760" # The conspirators get the man inside
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7762 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7760" # Hire killer
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7772 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7760" # Hire killer
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7772 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7760" # Knows the man for the job
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {

		}

					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7770 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7760" # Knows the man for the job
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
		}

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
			character_event = { id = 7770 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					character = ROOT

# Prison Break - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7766
	desc = "EVTDESC7766"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7766"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Prison Break - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7768
	desc = "EVTDESC7768"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7768"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7773"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Bathtub Drowning
character_event = {
	id = 7780
	desc = "EVTDESC7780"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			trait = incapable
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {

		}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

			plot_power = 0.5

			plot_power = 1.5

	option = {

		}

		}

			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }

		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7785 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7785" } }
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10

				prisoner = no

					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }

				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

# Bathtub Drowning - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7785
	desc = "EVTDESC7785"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7785" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}

				}

						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7787 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}

						factor = 1.33

character_event = {
	id = 7786
	desc = "EVTDESC7786"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7786"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7788
	desc = "EVTDESC7788"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7788"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7793
	desc = "EVTDESC7793"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

### BOATING ACCIDENT - CHILDREN ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Boating Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7800
	desc = "EVTDESC7800"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character

				age = 5

# Boating Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7805
	desc = "EVTDESC7805"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7805" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}

						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }

						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }

					character_event = { id = 7806 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}

					}
					character_event = { id = 7807 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			has_character_flag = murder_fail

		if = {

					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

						intrigue = 8
					}
