						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}

						factor = 1.33

# Boating Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7806
	desc = "EVTDESC7806"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7806"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boating Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7808
	desc = "EVTDESC7808"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7808"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boating Accident - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7813
	desc = "EVTDESC7813"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisonous Snake
character_event = {
	id = 7820
	desc = "EVTDESC7820"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {

		}

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7820" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7822 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7825" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7820" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			learning < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7832 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7825" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7820" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			learning < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7832 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7825" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7820" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			learning = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {

# Poisonous Snake - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7825
	desc = "EVTDESC7825"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7825" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7826 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7827 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7825" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7828 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7829 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisonous Snake - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7826
	desc = "EVTDESC7826"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7826"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_snakes
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_snakes
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisonous Snake - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7828
	desc = "EVTDESC7828"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7828"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7833
	desc = "EVTDESC7833"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7840
	desc = "EVTDESC7840"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
			is_nomadic = no
			NOT = { government = wildling_feudal_government }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

			}
		}

			}
		}
		modifier = {

				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7840" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7842 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7840" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue

			intrigue = 10

						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7850 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7840" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
		}

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
			character_event = { id = 7850 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}

# Balcony Plummet - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7846
	desc = "EVTDESC7846"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7846"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Balcony Plummet - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7848
	desc = "EVTDESC7848"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7848"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7853"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Hunting Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7860
	desc = "EVTDESC7860"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			NOT = { age = 16 }
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3600

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {

				power = 0.80
			}
		}

			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {

				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7860" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7862 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7865 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7865" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7860" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7872 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7865 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7865" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7860" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {

			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7865 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7865" } }

					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}

				plot_power_contribution = {

					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Hunting Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7865
	desc = "EVTDESC7865"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7865" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7866 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7867 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7865" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75

# Hunting Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7866
	desc = "EVTDESC7866"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7866"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hunting Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7868
	desc = "EVTDESC7868"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7868"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7873
	desc = "EVTDESC7873"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

	desc = "EVTDESC7875"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7875"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Disguised Highwaymen
character_event = {
	id = 7880
	desc = "EVTDESC7880"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {

				power = 0.10

		}

			plot_power = 1.0

			plot_power = 1.5

			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7880" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}

					character_event = { id = 7882 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7885 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7885" } }
	}

		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7885 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7885" } }
	}

		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5

			intrigue < 10

			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion

# Disguised Highwaymen - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7885
	desc = "EVTDESC7885"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7885" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7886 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7887 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7885" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {

# Disguised Highwaymen - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7886
	desc = "EVTDESC7886"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7886"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Dies, murderer NOT discovered

		if = {

						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7888
	desc = "EVTDESC7888"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7888"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7893
	desc = "EVTDESC7893"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

### CARRIAGE ACCIDENT
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Carriage Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7900
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7900" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7902 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			intrigue < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7900" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}

# Carriage Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7905
	desc = "EVTDESC7905"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7905" # Drowns
		trigger = {

# Carriage Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7906
	desc = "EVTDESC7906"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7906"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Carriage Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7908
	desc = "EVTDESC7908"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7908"
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8215
	desc = EVTDESC8215

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_increase_council_power }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_increase_council_power
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					is_republic = yes
					government = alliance_government
					is_nomadic = yes
					is_tribal = yes
				}
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 1 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
				who = ROOT
				months = 12
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 8217 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8218 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power
					letter_event = { id = 8216 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
		FROM = {
			faction_increase_council_power = { # The target (title) of the faction
				increase_council_power_effect = yes
				#break this breaks
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					is_republic = yes
					government = alliance_government
					is_nomadic = yes
					is_tribal = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				primary_title = { has_law = law_voting_power_0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
						trait = just
						FROM = { #aggressive expansion
							relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
							any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 2.0 } }
			}

			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8219 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {

						}
						20 = {

##Loyal councillor ends siege
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.13
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.13"

	picture = "GFX_evt_siege"
	border = "GFX_event_normal_frame_war"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		siege = {
			is_attacker = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			any_courtier_or_vassal = {
				is_councillor = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
				owes_favor_to = ROOT
				NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
				in_command = no
				ai = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			FROM = {
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					is_councillor = yes
					OR = {
						has_job_title = job_castellan
						has_job_title = job_marshal
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					owes_favor_to = ROOT
					NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
					in_command = no
					ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			FROM = {
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					is_councillor = yes
					has_job_title = job_physician
					liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					owes_favor_to = ROOT
					NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
					in_command = no
					ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			FROM = {
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					is_councillor = yes
					has_job_title = job_chancellor
					liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					owes_favor_to = ROOT
					NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
					in_command = no
					ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				OR = {
					has_job_title = job_castellan
					has_job_title = job_marshal
					has_job_title = job_spymaster
				}
				liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
				owes_favor_to = ROOT
				NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
				in_command = no
				ai = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = bought_councillor
			break = yes
		}
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				has_job_title = job_physician
				liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
				owes_favor_to = ROOT
				NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
				in_command = no
				ai = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = bought_councillor
			break = yes
		}
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				has_job_title = job_chancellor
				liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
				owes_favor_to = ROOT
				NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
				in_command = no
				ai = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = bought_councillor
			break = yes
		}
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT_FROM }
				owes_favor_to = ROOT
				NOT = { owes_favor_to = PREV }
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 50 } }
				in_command = no
				ai = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = bought_councillor
			break = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.13" #spymaster ends siege
		siege = {
			troops = -0.1
		}
		siege = {
			enemy = {
				morale = -10
				troops = -0.75
			}
		}
		remove_favor = event_target:bought_councillor
		event_target:bought_councillor = { prestige = 20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

#Bought character is asked to improve liege relations
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.16
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.16"
	picture = GFX_evt_council

	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes

	trigger = {
		owes_favor_to = FROMFROM
		liege = { ai = yes }
	}

	option = {  #will do
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.16"
		reverse_remove_favor = FROMFROM
		liege = {
			character_event = { id = plot_event.17  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.17" }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_opinion = { who = FROMFROM modifier = opinion_favored_being_called } }
	}
}
#attempts to convince liege plotter is a good guy
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.17
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.17"
	picture = GFX_evt_council

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		FROM = { is_alive = yes }
		FROMFROMFROM = { is_alive = yes }
	}

	option = {  #I'm convinced
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.17"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { diplomacy = 12 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { diplomacy = 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { diplomacy = 18 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { diplomacy = 21 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { diplomacy = 24 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.19 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.19" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROMFROM = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.20 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {  #I suppose he's OK
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.17"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				FROM = { diplomacy = 12 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				FROM = { diplomacy = 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				FROM = { diplomacy = 18 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				FROM = { diplomacy = 21 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				FROM = { diplomacy = 24 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.21 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.19" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROMFROM = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.22 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {  #I' don't think so
		name = "EVTOPTCplot_event.17"

			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -75
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -50
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -25
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = { FROM = { diplomacy = 9 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = { FROM = { diplomacy = 6 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = { FROM = { diplomacy = 3 } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.23 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.23" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {

			}
		}

#Bought character is asked to sabotage their job action
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.32
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.32"
	picture = GFX_evt_council

	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes

	trigger = {
		owes_favor_to = FROMFROM
	}

	option = {  #will do
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.16"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = 75 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = -50 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROMFROM value = -75 } }
			}
		}
		reverse_remove_favor = FROMFROM
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_opinion = { who = FROMFROM modifier = opinion_favored_being_called } }
		FROMFROM = { letter_event = { id = plot_event.33 } }
		add_character_modifier = { name = job_action_sabotage duration = 1825 } #stat penalty
		if = {
			limit = { has_job_action = action_improve_relations }
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						is_priest = no
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 20110 days = 10 random = 5 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20110" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_job_action = action_sow_dissent }
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
						independent = no
					}
					character_event = { id = 20170 days = 10 random = 5 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20170" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_job_action = action_statecraft }
			character_event = { id = 91096 days = 10 random = 5 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP91096" }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_squeeze_peasants
					has_job_action = action_oversee_province
				}
			}
			location = {
				# Inform barons about the rebels
				any_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						ai = no
					}
					character_event = { id = 20215 days = 10 random = 5 }
				}
				# Inform liege
				ROOT = {
					liege = { letter_event = { id = 20216 days = 10 random = 5 } }
					clr_character_flag = liege_informed
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_oversee_construction
					#has_job_action = action_advance_eco_tech
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 20242 days = 10 random = 5 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20242a" } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_administer_realm
					has_job_action = action_oversee_province
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = MNM.78007 days = 10 random = 5 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPMNM.78007" }

			}
			location = {

		if = {

				has_job_action = action_serve_court
			}
			liege = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						age = 6
						NOT = { age = 16 }

							character = PREV
							AND = {
								same_liege = ROOT
								is_close_relative = PREV
							}
						}
						is_incapable = no
						NOT = { trait = dragon }

					random_list = {
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_intrigue }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_stewardship }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_diplomacy  }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_learning  }
					}
					if = { limit = { NOT = { personality_traits = 5 } }
						random_list = {
							75 = { }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_slothful }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_wroth  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_proud  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_arbitrary  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_gluttonous  }

					}

				}
			}

		if = {

			}

			}
		}
	}

				who = ROOT

character_event = { #success
	id = plot_event.311
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.311"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	show_from_from_from = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:plot_target = { is_alive = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.311"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPplot_event.311
			hidden_tooltip = {
				event_target:plot_target = {
					#find plot to reveal
					random_unknown_plotter = {
						limit = {
							plot_target_char = { always = yes }
							NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
							NOT = { plot_is_known_by = event_target:plot_target }
							NOT = { character = event_target:plot_target }
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							same_realm = ROOT
						}
						set_character_flag = bought_councillor_reveal
						character_event = { id = 20290 }
						break = yes
					}
					random_close_relative = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								dynasty = event_target:plot_target
								is_child_of = event_target:plot_target
								is_grandchild_of = event_target:plot_target
								is_parent_of = event_target:plot_target
								is_grandparent_of = event_target:plot_target
								sibling = event_target:plot_target
							}
							any_unknown_plotter = {
								plot_target_char = { always = yes }
								NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
								NOT = { plot_is_known_by = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								same_realm = ROOT
							}
						}
						random_unknown_plotter = {
							limit = {
								plot_target_char = { always = yes }
								NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
								NOT = { plot_is_known_by = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								same_realm = ROOT
							}
							set_character_flag = bought_councillor_reveal
							character_event = { id = 20290 }
							break = yes
						}
					}
					random_spouse = {
						limit = {
							any_unknown_plotter = {
								plot_target_char = { always = yes }
								NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
								NOT = { plot_is_known_by = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = event_target:plot_target }
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								same_realm = ROOT
							}
						}
						random_unknown_plotter = {
							limit = {
								plot_target_char = { always = yes }
								NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
								NOT = { plot_is_known_by = event_target:plot_target }

							}

character_event = { #Inform ROOT
	id = plot_event.322
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.322"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.322"
		tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = -5 } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 9.9 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				change_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = -5 }
			}
			if = { #recalculate tyranny trait
				limit = { NOT = { trait = tyrannical_stain } }
				character_event = { id = maintenance.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = "tyrant" value = 0.9 } }
				}
				remove_trait = tyrannical_stain
			}
		}
	}
}

#iKigndoms are revoked until less than 3 are held
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.349

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { num_of_king_titles = 3 }
			random_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = KING
					can_be_given_away = yes
					is_primary_holder_title = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holder_scope = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } } }
					usurp_title = FROMFROM
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = kingdom_found }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { NOT = { has_character_flag = kingdom_found } }
						holder_scope = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					usurp_title = FROM
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = kingdom_found }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = kingdom_found
					num_of_king_titles = 3
				}
				clr_character_flag = kingdom_found
				repeat_event = { id = plot_event.349 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
# Vassal believes his liege should make him Lord Paramount
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.37
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.37"
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	border = "GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	war = no

	trigger = {
		independent = no
		is_nomadic = no
		NOT = { is_military_command_trigger = yes }
		tier = DUKE
		can_press_claims_trigger = yes
		is_theocracy = no
		NAND = {
			liege = { is_valyrian_freehold_trigger = yes }
			government = feudal_government_LP
		}
		liege = {
			tier = EMPEROR
			OR = {
				any_vassal = { tier = KING }
				num_of_king_titles = 2
			}
			NOT =  { #Interregnum
				primary_title = {
					is_variable_equal = { which = "lord_paramount_status" value = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		primary_title = {
			dejure_liege_title = {
				NOT = { any_war = { always = yes } } #is not being contested
				OR = { #is either vacant or held by liege
					has_holder = no
					holder_scope = {
						is_liege_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = { #Cannot ask for primary LP title
					holder_scope = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = count
							location = { is_capital = yes }
							de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				NAND = {  #Cannot ask for sole LP title in Iron Throne elective realm
					holder_scope = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
					dejure_liege_title = {
						title = e_iron_throne
						NOT = { has_global_flag = non_iron_throne_westeros }
						has_elective_law_trigger = yes
						holder_scope = {
							is_liege_of = ROOT
							NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				OR = { #Must hold title or control all the territory
					holder_scope = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
					ROOT = { liege = { completely_controls = PREVPREV } }
					NOT = {
						any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
							holder_scope = {
								NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
								NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = { #cannot request a vacant crownlands title
					NOT = { title = k_crownlands }
					has_holder = yes
				}
				OR = { #Cannot request Sarnor or North Valyria if they have had no previous holder
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							title = k_sarnor
							title = k_north_valyria
							title = k_long_summer
						}
					}
					any_previous_holder = { always = yes }
				}
				OR = { #Can only request Andalos or Rhoyne if correct culture
					NOT = { title = k_andalos }
					ROOT = { culture_group = andal }
				}
				OR = { #Can only request Andalos or Rhoyne if correct culture
					NOT = { title = k_rhoynar }
					ROOT = { culture_group = dornish }
				}
				NOT = { #cannot request a title if equivalent kingdom exists
					OR = {
						title = k_nightswatch
						AND = {
							title = k_north
							e_north = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_riverlands
							e_riverlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_vale
							e_vale = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_westerlands
							e_westerlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_reach
							e_reach = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_stormlands
							e_stormlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_dorne
							e_dorne = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_iron_isles
							e_iron_isles = { has_holder = yes }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = requested_lord_paramountcy }
			had_character_flag = { flag = requested_lord_paramountcy days = 3650 }
		}
	}

	immediate = { primary_title = { dejure_liege_title = { save_event_target_as = LP_title } } }#for loc

	option = {

			modifier = {

				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 15
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 30
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 50
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 75
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = humble
			}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7507"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_title = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						dynasty = ROOT
						any_backed_character = {
							character = ROOT
							has_plot = plot_dynasty_claim
						}
						OR = {
							has_strong_claim = PREVPREV
							AND = {
								has_weak_claim = PREVPREV
								OR = {
									FROM = { has_regent = yes }
									AND = {
										is_female = no
										FROM = { is_female = yes }
									}
									ROOT = { plot_target_title = { is_contested = yes } } # Is already being contested in some form of Claim or Succession War
									FROM = { trait = bastard }
									FROM = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = dynasty_claim_target
				}
			}
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = dynasty_plot_claim
				plot_backers = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7507"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -100
		any_plot_backer = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coward
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				letter_event = { id = 8120 }
			}
		}

	}

# Ultimatum - Depose Liege (AGOT)
letter_event = {
	id = plot_event.42
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.42"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_depose_liege }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_depose_liege
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				capital_scope = {
					has_title_flag = major_capital
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = {
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								trait = just
								FROM = { #aggressive expansion
									relative_power = { who = ROOT power = 1.5 }
									any_claim = { holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_player = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT

						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						war_with = ROOT
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant }
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						FROM = { any_faction_backer = { character = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.45 }
			}
			FROM = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_depose_liege
					letter_event = { id = plot_event.44 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.43 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
