# Demand accepted - Depose Liege
letter_event = {
	id = plot_event.43
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.43"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			current_heir = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_very_grateful
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
				reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_depose_liege_ultimatum_taken
		FROM = {
			# mark titles for claims
			primary_title = {
				set_title_flag = depose_liege_claims
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { tier = ROOT_FROM }
				set_title_flag = depose_liege_claims
			}
			if = { #Triarch for life, revert to default law
				limit = {
					primary_title = { has_law = republic_triarch_for_life }
					ROOT = { NOT = { has_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life } }
				}
				family_palace = {
					current_heir = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life
							}
							clr_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life
							remove_title = title_triarch_for_life
						}
					}
				}
				primary_title = { add_law = republic_law_0 }
			}
			if = { #Night's watch versus Night's king, dethrone
				limit = {
					ROOT = { trait = nightswatch }
					has_landed_title = k_nightswatch
				}
				set_character_flag = destroy_nights_king
				tooltip = { k_nightswatch = { destroy_landed_title = THIS } }
			}
			current_heir = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						prisoner = yes
						host = { character = FROM  }
					}
					prisoner = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = deposed_heir
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = no }
				current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
				family_palace = { current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir } }
			}
			transfer_scaled_wealth = { to = event_target:wealth_heir value = all }
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = no }
				hidden_tooltip = { #Universal on death/abdication event
					if = {
						limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					}
					set_character_flag = abdication
					character_event = { id = 45341 }
					clr_character_flag = abdication
					#clr_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
				}
				abdicate = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
				character_event = { id = REP.903 tooltip = TOOLTIPREP.903B } #Hold Election
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no
					liege = { NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT } }
				}
				event_target:deposed_heir = { reverse_banish = PREV }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = deposed_AGOT
				duration = 3650
			}
			event_target:deposed_heir = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { has_title_flag = depose_liege_claims }
					add_pressed_claim = ROOT_FROM
					clr_title_flag = depose_liege_claims
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { #make sure kingdom is transferred in merchant republic
			top_liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_merchant_republic = yes
						tier = EMPEROR
					}
					capital_scope = {
						kingdom = {
							if = {
								limit = { holder = FROM }
								gain_title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### BODYGUARD ASSASINATION
# The plotter sees an opportunity - BODYGUARD
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.50
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.50"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_ruler = yes
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_liege_of = ROOT
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
							has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
							trait = kingsguard
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_landed_title = d_kingsguard }
				}
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = e_iron_throne
					ROOT = { trait = kingsguard }
				}
			}
			prisoner = no
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = {
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.44
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			plot_power = 2.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			plot_target_char = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.50" # The conspirator has plot power
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.50" # Bribes
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			martial < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -1.5 min = -20 max = -150 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.50" # Bribes
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			martial < 10
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.5 min = -10 max = -100 }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCplot_event.50" # Knows the right moment
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			intrigue < 10
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}

character_event = {

	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				age = 16
				is_ruler = yes
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_liege_of = ROOT
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
								has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
								trait = kingsguard
							}
						}
						NOT = { has_landed_title = d_kingsguard }
					}
					AND = {
						has_landed_title = e_iron_throne
						ROOT = { trait = kingsguard }
					}
				}
				prisoner = no
			}
			OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { trait = honorable }
		NOT = { trait = honest }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.10
					}

		}

			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

# BODYGUARD  - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.54
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.54"
	picture = "GFX_evt_shadow"
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.54" # Felled
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						intrigue < 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { intrigue < 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75

					}
					character_event = { id = plot_event.56 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

				limit = {

						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no

						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						NOR = {
							war_with = ROOT
							any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {

						intrigue < 2

					}

					modifier = {

						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {

# BODYGUARD  - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.55
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.55"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		kingsguard = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				move_character = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { trait = kingsguard }
					remove_trait = kingsguard
					add_trait = former_kingsguard
				}
				clr_character_flag = no_court_invites
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bodyguard }
				remove_title = title_bodyguard
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bloodrider }
				remove_title = title_bloodrider
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.55"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# BODYGUARD  - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.57
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.57"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
				save_event_target_as = imprison_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.57"
		kingsguard = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				move_character = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { trait = kingsguard }
					remove_trait = kingsguard
					add_trait = former_kingsguard
				}
				clr_character_flag = no_court_invites
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bodyguard }
				remove_title = title_bodyguard
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bloodrider }
				remove_title = title_bloodrider
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = trusting }
				NOT = { trait = paranoid }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38275 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trusting }
			remove_trait = trusting
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = alerted_to_plot
			duration = 1095
		}
		event_target:imprison_target = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			any_liege = {
				limit = {
					ai = yes
					OR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
					}
					NOT = { character = event_target:imprison_target }
				}
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 1 random = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = "GFX_evt_shadow"
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}

### PEACE BANNER ATTACK
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Peace Banner Attack
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.66
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.66"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_playable = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		war = yes
		plot_target_char = {
			is_ruler = yes
			war = yes
			any_current_enemy = { character = ROOT }
			age = 16
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			in_command = yes
			NOT = { is_at_sea = yes }
			OR = { #Must be losing in the war
				any_war = {
					attacker = { character = ROOT }
					defender = { character = PREVPREV }
					NOT = { war_score = -50 }
				}
				any_war = {
					defender = { character = ROOT }
					attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
					war_score = 50
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
					had_character_flag = { flag = murder_in_motion days = 100 }
				}
		plot_power_contribution = {
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
		NOT = { trait = honorable }
		NOT = { trait = honest }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power = 0.55
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.66" # Do it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				plot_target_char = {
					OR = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = { trait = ruthless }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.70 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.67 days = 15 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.67" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.66" # Not this way

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = kind
			}
		}
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.67
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.67"
	picture = GFX_evt_courier
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
			is_ruler = yes
			war = yes
		}
		is_ruler = yes
		war = yes
		any_current_enemy = { character = FROM }
	}

	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.67" # Killed
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = plot_event.68 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.67" # Not killed
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = plot_event.69 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
		}
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.68
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.68"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.68"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = yes }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}
				tooltip = { death = yes }
				save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
			kingsguard = {
				limit = {
					is_alive = yes
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
					NOR = {
						war_with = ROOT
						any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				tooltip = { death = yes }
				save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
			tooltip = { death = yes }
			save_event_target_as = slayed_courtier
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.71 } } }
		death = {
			death_reason = death_murder_slayed
			killer = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.69
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.69"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = {
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.69"
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
			tooltip = { death = yes }
			save_event_target_as = slayed_courtier
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = yes }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { }
					20 = { add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes }
					20 = { add_trait = maimed }
					20 = {
						tooltip = { death = yes }
						save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
			kingsguard = {
				limit = {
					is_alive = yes
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
					NOR = {
						war_with = ROOT
						any_liege = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { }
					20 = { add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes }
					20 = { add_trait = maimed }
					20 = {
						tooltip = { death = yes }
						save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.72 } } }
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.71
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.71"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						same_realm = FROM
						primary_title = {
							OR = {
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
								FROM = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = plot_event.73 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		FROM = {
			tooltip = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_murder_slayed
					killer = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:slayed_bodyguard = {
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		event_target:slayed_courtier = {
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		piety = -200
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honest }
			remove_trait = honest
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = honorable }
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cutthroat_religion_trigger = yes } }
			tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 } }
		}
	}
}
